gpg --home-dir gpg-dir --list-keys

gpg --homedir gpg-dir \

BGP is intending to use the protocol which has the vulnerabilities that you analysed in task 2 as part of its wireless maintenance mode. You are to: 
Task 3.1) Critically analyse the available spectrum and recommend the most appropriate part of the spectrum to be used for wireless maintenance.  
Task 3.2) Select plausible antennae to utilise both on the turbines and by the mobile maintenance teams.  
Task 3.3) Model how the antenna would be positioned / oriented. Make reasonable, explicit simplifying assumptions to maximise the value of the models in the limited time that you have available to develop them. 
Task 3.4) Recommend and rank the most significant cyber controls that BGP should put in place in order to minimise the cyber risk of operating the protocol over wireless, using the spectrum and antennae that you recommend. 
Task 3.5) Recommend the most appropriate modulation scheme to utilise. The evidence for the selection should be brief but clear, allowing the reader quickly to grasp the rationale for the rejection of alternatives.
